néedes die without anie hope remedie would haue procéeded cardina stepped saluted said secretelie princesse griana sent vnderstand health beléeue good prince quoth neuer sawe ladie sorrowfull sicknes commendeth selfe honour hartilie hath sent ring earnest looue beares desiring bee good chéere comfort selfe desire sée confer matter concerne bothe néerelie wordes rauished spirit florendos good doubted whether dreamed hee might giue credite hearde albeit knewe messenger well anie courte yet coulde perswade himselfe hee fortunate length betwéene hope dispayre tooke ring entertained manie deuoute ky embracing cardina well hee coulde thus answered ala swéete fréende may bee possible ladie hath regard neuer able doo anie seruice doubt thereof lorde aunswered cardina declare loue answerable vertue must giue testimonie thereof comforting person may sée soone may ah fayre uirgin quoth let whole life imployed shall like diuine nature cō maunde assure tydings hath breathed newe life verie soule alreadie finde selfe wonderfullie chaunged yea sorte thrée day bee past shall attende gracious seruiceable dilligence meane shal desire faire fréend let soueraigne mistresse
